SCOPE NOTES:
  - strategies.json contains 15 strategies, not 19 as requested.
  - support_resistance: SKIPPED. Discretionary/manual S&R levels,
    intraday 5m chart — not mechanically backtestable on daily bars,
    and not in the user's own numbered strategy list either.
  - death_cross: SKIPPED. Short-only signal with no long-only
    equivalent (established in this project's backtest.sh already).
  - dow_theory: run SEPARATELY on NIFTY (^NSEI) and SENSEX (^BSESN)
    only, using weekly bars — see dedicated section below. Not run
    against individual stocks per strategy_selector.md's own rule
    ("Do not use Dow Theory on individual stocks").
  - bollinger_bands: run using the MEAN-REVERSION rule (buy at lower
    band, sell at middle/upper) — the rule actually documented in
    strategies.json, not the breakout variant used in an earlier
    one-off ASIANPAINT-specific test.

12 strategies actually run across all 25 stocks: SMA 80, EMA 80,
SMA 5, SMA 30, MACD 26-12-9, RSI 14, Bollinger Bands 20-2
(mean-reversion), Golden Cross, Bullish Engulfing, Bullish Harami,
Morning Star, Piercing Pattern.
